Candidate  Screening  Interview  
 
Executive  Summary:   This  quick  screening  interview  is  designed  to  assess  candidate  seriousness,  
availability,
 
and
 
reliability
 
within
 
5
 
minutes.
 
Use
 
this
 
checklist
 
before
 
forwarding
 
candidates
 
to
 
clients.
 
Questions:  
1.  Are  you  currently  working?  If  yes,  have  you  resigned?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I  have  resigned"  or  "No,  I’m  available  
immediately"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "Still  working  but  haven’t  informed  my  employer"  
 2.  What  is  your  exact  joining  availability?  a.  Expected  Answer:  A  speciﬁc  date  within  the  required  timeline,  example:  
"I
 
can
 
join
 
on
 
or
 
before
 
5th
 
August"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "It  depends..."  or  vague  responses  
 3.  Have  you  discussed  this  opportunity  with  your  family  or  dependents?  Are  they  
supportive?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  they  support  my  decision"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Not  yet"  or  visible  hesitation  
 4.  Have  you  applied  elsewhere  or  do  you  have  other  offers  pending?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "No,  I  am  focused  on  this  opportunity"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Yes,  I  have  multiple  offers  and  waiting  to  decide"  
 5.  Are  you  fully  committed  to  joining  this  job  if  selected?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  100%  committed"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  conﬁrm  after  selection"  or  uncertainty

6.  Are  you  ready  to  relocate  and  work  under  the  offered  conditions  
(accommodation,
 
food,
 
shifts)?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I’m  okay  with  the  terms"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  see  after  selection"  or  conditional  acceptance  
 7.  Are  your  documents  ready  —  valid  passport,  certiﬁcates,  etc.?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  all  documents  are  ready"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I  need  to  arrange  them"  or  "Not  sure  if  all  are  valid"  
 
Wrap-Up  Line:   
“Thanks.
 
If
 
selected,
 
would
 
you
 
be
 
willing
 
to
 
sign
 
a
 
short
 
commitment
 
letter
 
conﬁrming
 
your
 
intent
 
to
 
join?”
 
(This
 
is
 
not
 
legally
 
binding,
 
but
 
it
 
helps
 
reinforce
 
commitment.)

About Us
Who We Are
COTER Global is a specialized Health, Safety & Environment (HSE) consultancy, training,
and recruitment firm dedicated to helping organizations build safer workplaces. We deliver
industry-aligned safety solutions, accredited training, and experienced HSE personnel to
support compliance, risk reduction, and operational continuity across construction, oil &
gas, manufacturing, facilities management, and other high-risk sectors in the UAE and
beyond.
In addition to consultancy and training, COTER Global provides specialized recruitment
services for qualified Occupational Health and Safety (OHSE) professionals, including HSE
Managers, Engineers, Officers, and Advisors. Our recruitment division focuses on
connecting top-tier safety professionals with leading organizations, ensuring the right
expertise is deployed to meet project and corporate HSE requirements effectively.
Cover About Us Services Contact Us

Cover About Us Services Contact Us
OUR MISSION
To empower industries by delivering
specialized recruitment solutions that
connect them with qualified Occupational
Health, Safety, and Environment (OHSE)
professionals, helping organizations build
safer, compliant, and more resilient
workplaces.
OUR VISION
To be a global leader in specialized HSE
recruitment, recognized for connecting
industries with top Occupational Health
and Safety professionals and contributing
to safer, more sustainable, and high-
performing workplaces worldwide.

Meet Our Team
At COTER Global, our people are more than professionals - they are safety and business partners.  
Together, they deliver reliable expertise that protects, empowers, and grows your workforce.

We recruit qualified HSE professionals with proven expertise in safety, compliance, and
environmental management — covering all positions from HSE Assistants to OHSE Directors.
Our candidates are ready to integrate seamlessly into your operations, delivering immediate
value by strengthening safety culture, sustainability, and overall performance.

and

within

immediately"

"I

on
 
or
 
before
 
5th
 
August"

About Us
Who We Are
COTER Global is a specialized Health, Safety & Environment (HSE) consultancy, training,
and recruitment firm dedicated to helping organizations build safer workplaces. We deliver
industry-aligned safety solutions, accredited training, and experienced HSE personnel to
support compliance, risk reduction, and operational continuity across construction, oil &
gas, manufacturing, facilities management, and other high-risk sectors in the UAE and
beyond.
In addition to consultancy and training, COTER Global provides specialized recruitment
services for qualified Occupational Health and Safety (OHSE) professionals, including HSE
Managers, Engineers, Officers, and Advisors. Our recruitment division focuses on
connecting top-tier safety professionals with leading organizations, ensuring the right
expertise is deployed to meet project and corporate HSE requirements effectively.
Cover About Us Services Contact Us

Cover About Us Services Contact Us
OUR MISSION
To empower industries by delivering
specialized recruitment solutions that
connect them with qualified Occupational
Health, Safety, and Environment (OHSE)
professionals, helping organizations build
safer, compliant, and more resilient
workplaces.
OUR VISION
To be a global leader in specialized HSE
recruitment, recognized for connecting
industries with top Occupational Health
and Safety professionals and contributing
to safer, more sustainable, and high-
performing workplaces worldwide.

We recruit qualified HSE professionals with proven expertise in safety, compliance, and
environmental management — covering all positions from HSE Assistants to OHSE Directors.
Our candidates are ready to integrate seamlessly into your operations, delivering immediate
value by strengthening safety culture, sustainability, and overall performance.

Additional Information



Candidate  Screening  Interview  
 
Executive  Summary:   This  quick  screening  interview  is  designed  to  assess  candidate  seriousness,  
availability,
 
and
 
reliability
 
within
 
5
 
minutes.
 
Use
 
this
 
checklist
 
before
 
forwarding
 
candidates
 
to
 
clients.
 
Questions:  
1.  Are  you  currently  working?  If  yes,  have  you  resigned?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I  have  resigned"  or  "No,  I’m  available  
immediately"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "Still  working  but  haven’t  informed  my  employer"  
 2.  What  is  your  exact  joining  availability?  a.  Expected  Answer:  A  speciﬁc  date  within  the  required  timeline,  example:  
"I
 
can
 
join
 
on
 
or
 
before
 
5th
 
August"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "It  depends..."  or  vague  responses  
 3.  Have  you  discussed  this  opportunity  with  your  family  or  dependents?  Are  they  
supportive?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  they  support  my  decision"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Not  yet"  or  visible  hesitation  
 4.  Have  you  applied  elsewhere  or  do  you  have  other  offers  pending?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "No,  I  am  focused  on  this  opportunity"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Yes,  I  have  multiple  offers  and  waiting  to  decide"  
 5.  Are  you  fully  committed  to  joining  this  job  if  selected?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  100%  committed"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  conﬁrm  after  selection"  or  uncertainty

6.  Are  you  ready  to  relocate  and  work  under  the  offered  conditions  
(accommodation,
 
food,
 
shifts)?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I’m  okay  with  the  terms"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  see  after  selection"  or  conditional  acceptance  
 7.  Are  your  documents  ready  —  valid  passport,  certiﬁcates,  etc.?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  all  documents  are  ready"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I  need  to  arrange  them"  or  "Not  sure  if  all  are  valid"  
 
Wrap-Up  Line:   
“Thanks.
 
If
 
selected,
 
would
 
you
 
be
 
willing
 
to
 
sign
 
a
 
short
 
commitment
 
letter
 
conﬁrming
 
your

to

About Us
Who We Are
COTER Global is a specialized Health, Safety & Environment (HSE) consultancy, training,
and recruitment firm dedicated to helping organizations build safer workplaces. We deliver
industry-aligned safety solutions, accredited training, and experienced HSE personnel to
support compliance, risk reduction, and operational continuity across construction, oil &
gas, manufacturing, facilities management, and other high-risk sectors in the UAE and
beyond.
In addition to consultancy and training, COTER Global provides specialized recruitment
services for qualified Occupational Health and Safety (OHSE) professionals, including HSE
Managers, Engineers, Officers, and Advisors. Our recruitment division focuses on
connecting top-tier safety professionals with leading organizations, ensuring the right
expertise is deployed to meet project and corporate HSE requirements effectively.
Cover About Us Services Contact Us

Cover About Us Services Contact Us
OUR MISSION
To empower industries by delivering
specialized recruitment solutions that
connect them with qualified Occupational
Health, Safety, and Environment (OHSE)
professionals, helping organizations build
safer, compliant, and more resilient
workplaces.
OUR VISION
To be a global leader in specialized HSE
recruitment, recognized for connecting
industries with top Occupational Health
and Safety professionals and contributing
to safer, more sustainable, and high-
performing workplaces worldwide.

Meet Our Team
At COTER Global, our people are more than professionals - they are safety and business partners.  
Together, they deliver reliable expertise that protects, empowers, and grows your workforce.

We recruit qualified HSE professionals with proven expertise in safety, compliance, and
environmental management — covering all positions from HSE Assistants to OHSE Directors.
Our candidates are ready to integrate seamlessly into your operations, delivering immediate
value by strengthening safety culture, sustainability, and overall performance.

Executive  Summary:   This  quick  screening  interview  is  designed  to  assess  candidate  seriousness,  
availability,
 
and
 
reliability
 
within
 
5
 
minutes.

this
 
checklist
 
before
 
forwarding
 
candidates
 
to
 
clients.
 
Questions:  
1.  Are  you  currently  working?  If  yes,  have  you  resigned?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I  have  resigned"  or  "No,  I’m  available  
immediately"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "Still  working  but  haven’t  informed  my  employer"  
 2.  What  is  your  exact  joining  availability?  a.  Expected  Answer:  A  speciﬁc  date  within  the  required  timeline,  example:  
"I
 
can
 
join
 
on
 
or
 
before
 
5th
 
August"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "It  depends..."  or  vague  responses  
 3.  Have  you  discussed  this  opportunity  with  your  family  or  dependents?  Are  they  
supportive?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  they  support  my  decision"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Not  yet"  or  visible  hesitation  
 4.  Have  you  applied  elsewhere  or  do  you  have  other  offers  pending?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "No,  I  am  focused  on  this  opportunity"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Yes,  I  have  multiple  offers  and  waiting  to  decide"

6.  Are  you  ready  to  relocate  and  work  under  the  offered  conditions  
(accommodation,
 
food,
 
shifts)?

 7.  Are  your  documents  ready  —  valid  passport,  certiﬁcates,  etc.?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  all  documents  are  ready"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I  need  to  arrange  them"  or  "Not  sure  if  all  are  valid"

About Us
Who We Are
COTER Global is a specialized Health, Safety & Environment (HSE) consultancy, training,
and recruitment firm dedicated to helping organizations build safer workplaces. We deliver
industry-aligned safety solutions, accredited training, and experienced HSE personnel to
support compliance, risk reduction, and operational continuity across construction, oil &
gas, manufacturing, facilities management, and other high-risk sectors in the UAE and
beyond.
In addition to consultancy and training, COTER Global provides specialized recruitment
services for qualified Occupational Health and Safety (OHSE) professionals, including HSE
Managers, Engineers, Officers, and Advisors. Our recruitment division focuses on
connecting top-tier safety professionals with leading organizations, ensuring the right
expertise is deployed to meet project and corporate HSE requirements effectively.

Additional Information



Candidate  Screening  Interview  
 
Executive  Summary:   This  quick  screening  interview  is  designed  to  assess  candidate  seriousness,  
availability,
 
and
 
reliability
 
within
 
5
 
minutes.
 
Use
 
this
 
checklist
 
before
 
forwarding
 
candidates
 
to
 
clients.
 
Questions:  
1.  Are  you  currently  working?  If  yes,  have  you  resigned?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I  have  resigned"  or  "No,  I’m  available  
immediately"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "Still  working  but  haven’t  informed  my  employer"  
 2.  What  is  your  exact  joining  availability?  a.  Expected  Answer:  A  speciﬁc  date  within  the  required  timeline,  example:  
"I
 
can
 
join
 
on
 
or
 
before
 
5th
 
August"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "It  depends..."  or  vague  responses  
 3.  Have  you  discussed  this  opportunity  with  your  family  or  dependents?  Are  they  
supportive?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  they  support  my  decision"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Not  yet"  or  visible  hesitation  
 4.  Have  you  applied  elsewhere  or  do  you  have  other  offers  pending?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "No,  I  am  focused  on  this  opportunity"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Yes,  I  have  multiple  offers  and  waiting  to  decide"  
 5.  Are  you  fully  committed  to  joining  this  job  if  selected?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  100%  committed"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  conﬁrm  after  selection"  or  uncertainty

6.  Are  you  ready  to  relocate  and  work  under  the  offered  conditions  
(accommodation,
 
food,
 
shifts)?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I’m  okay  with  the  terms"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  see  after  selection"  or  conditional  acceptance  
 7.  Are  your  documents  ready  —  valid  passport,  certiﬁcates,  etc.?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  all  documents  are  ready"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I  need  to  arrange  them"  or  "Not  sure  if  all  are  valid"  
 
Wrap-Up  Line:   
“Thanks.
 
If
 
selected,
 
would
 
you
 
be
 
willing
 
to
 
sign
 
a
 
short
 
commitment
 
letter
 
conﬁrming
 
your
 
intent
 
to
 
join?”

About Us
Who We Are
COTER Global is a specialized Health, Safety & Environment (HSE) consultancy, training,
and recruitment firm dedicated to helping organizations build safer workplaces. We deliver
industry-aligned safety solutions, accredited training, and experienced HSE personnel to
support compliance, risk reduction, and operational continuity across construction, oil &
gas, manufacturing, facilities management, and other high-risk sectors in the UAE and
beyond.
In addition to consultancy and training, COTER Global provides specialized recruitment
services for qualified Occupational Health and Safety (OHSE) professionals, including HSE
Managers, Engineers, Officers, and Advisors. Our recruitment division focuses on
connecting top-tier safety professionals with leading organizations, ensuring the right
expertise is deployed to meet project and corporate HSE requirements effectively.
Cover About Us Services Contact Us

Cover About Us Services Contact Us
OUR MISSION
To empower industries by delivering
specialized recruitment solutions that
connect them with qualified Occupational
Health, Safety, and Environment (OHSE)
professionals, helping organizations build
safer, compliant, and more resilient
workplaces.
OUR VISION
To be a global leader in specialized HSE
recruitment, recognized for connecting
industries with top Occupational Health
and Safety professionals and contributing
to safer, more sustainable, and high-
performing workplaces worldwide.

Meet Our Team
At COTER Global, our people are more than professionals - they are safety and business partners.  
Together, they deliver reliable expertise that protects, empowers, and grows your workforce.

We recruit qualified HSE professionals with proven expertise in safety, compliance, and
environmental management — covering all positions from HSE Assistants to OHSE Directors.
Our candidates are ready to integrate seamlessly into your operations, delivering immediate
value by strengthening safety culture, sustainability, and overall performance.

and

within
 
5
 
minutes.

this

before
 
forwarding
 
candidates
 
to
 
clients.

1.  Are  you  currently  working?  If  yes,  have  you  resigned?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I  have  resigned"  or  "No,  I’m  available  
immediately"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "Still  working  but  haven’t  informed  my  employer"  
 2.  What  is  your  exact  joining  availability?  a.  Expected  Answer:  A  speciﬁc  date  within  the  required  timeline,  example:  
"I
 
can
 
join
 
on
 
or
 
before
 
5th
 
August"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "It  depends..."  or  vague  responses  
 3.  Have  you  discussed  this  opportunity  with  your  family  or  dependents?  Are  they  
supportive?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  they  support  my  decision"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Not  yet"  or  visible  hesitation  
 4.  Have  you  applied  elsewhere  or  do  you  have  other  offers  pending?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "No,  I  am  focused  on  this  opportunity"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Yes,  I  have  multiple  offers  and  waiting  to  decide"

6.  Are  you  ready  to  relocate  and  work  under  the  offered  conditions  
(accommodation,
 
food,
 
shifts)?

 7.  Are  your  documents  ready  —  valid  passport,  certiﬁcates,  etc.?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  all  documents  are  ready"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I  need  to  arrange  them"  or  "Not  sure  if  all  are  valid"

Meet Our Team
At COTER Global, our people are more than professionals - they are safety and business partners.  
Together, they deliver reliable expertise that protects, empowers, and grows your workforce.

We recruit qualified HSE professionals with proven expertise in safety, compliance, and
environmental management — covering all positions from HSE Assistants to OHSE Directors.
Our candidates are ready to integrate seamlessly into your operations, delivering immediate
value by strengthening safety culture, sustainability, and overall performance.

Additional Information



Candidate  Screening  Interview  
 
Executive  Summary:   This  quick  screening  interview  is  designed  to  assess  candidate  seriousness,  
availability,
 
and
 
reliability
 
within
 
5
 
minutes.
 
Use
 
this
 
checklist
 
before
 
forwarding
 
candidates
 
to
 
clients.
 
Questions:  
1.  Are  you  currently  working?  If  yes,  have  you  resigned?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I  have  resigned"  or  "No,  I’m  available  
immediately"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "Still  working  but  haven’t  informed  my  employer"  
 2.  What  is  your  exact  joining  availability?  a.  Expected  Answer:  A  speciﬁc  date  within  the  required  timeline,  example:  
"I
 
can
 
join
 
on
 
or
 
before
 
5th
 
August"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "It  depends..."  or  vague  responses  
 3.  Have  you  discussed  this  opportunity  with  your  family  or  dependents?  Are  they  
supportive?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  they  support  my  decision"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Not  yet"  or  visible  hesitation  
 4.  Have  you  applied  elsewhere  or  do  you  have  other  offers  pending?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "No,  I  am  focused  on  this  opportunity"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Yes,  I  have  multiple  offers  and  waiting  to  decide"  
 5.  Are  you  fully  committed  to  joining  this  job  if  selected?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  100%  committed"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  conﬁrm  after  selection"  or  uncertainty

6.  Are  you  ready  to  relocate  and  work  under  the  offered  conditions  
(accommodation,
 
food,
 
shifts)?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I’m  okay  with  the  terms"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  see  after  selection"  or  conditional  acceptance  
 7.  Are  your  documents  ready  —  valid  passport,  certiﬁcates,  etc.?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  all  documents  are  ready"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I  need  to  arrange  them"  or  "Not  sure  if  all  are  valid"  
 
Wrap-Up  Line:   
“Thanks.
 
If
 
selected,
 
would
 
you
 
be
 
willing
 
to
 
sign
 
a
 
short
 
commitment
 
letter
 
conﬁrming
 
your
 
intent
 
to
 
join?”
 
(This
 
is
 
not
 
legally
 
binding,
 
but
 
it
 
helps
 
reinforce
 
commitment.)

About Us
Who We Are
COTER Global is a specialized Health, Safety & Environment (HSE) consultancy, training,
and recruitment firm dedicated to helping organizations build safer workplaces. We deliver
industry-aligned safety solutions, accredited training, and experienced HSE personnel to
support compliance, risk reduction, and operational continuity across construction, oil &
gas, manufacturing, facilities management, and other high-risk sectors in the UAE and
beyond.
In addition to consultancy and training, COTER Global provides specialized recruitment
services for qualified Occupational Health and Safety (OHSE) professionals, including HSE
Managers, Engineers, Officers, and Advisors. Our recruitment division focuses on
connecting top-tier safety professionals with leading organizations, ensuring the right
expertise is deployed to meet project and corporate HSE requirements effectively.
Cover About Us Services Contact Us

Cover About Us Services Contact Us
OUR MISSION
To empower industries by delivering
specialized recruitment solutions that
connect them with qualified Occupational
Health, Safety, and Environment (OHSE)
professionals, helping organizations build
safer, compliant, and more resilient
workplaces.
OUR VISION
To be a global leader in specialized HSE
recruitment, recognized for connecting
industries with top Occupational Health
and Safety professionals and contributing
to safer, more sustainable, and high-
performing workplaces worldwide.

and

within

can
 
join
 
on
 
or
 
before
 
5th

 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I’m  okay  with  the  terms"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  see  after  selection"  or  conditional  acceptance  
 7.  Are  your  documents  ready  —  valid  passport,  certiﬁcates,  etc.?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  all  documents  are  ready"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I  need  to  arrange  them"  or  "Not  sure  if  all  are  valid"

About Us
Who We Are
COTER Global is a specialized Health, Safety & Environment (HSE) consultancy, training,
and recruitment firm dedicated to helping organizations build safer workplaces. We deliver
industry-aligned safety solutions, accredited training, and experienced HSE personnel to
support compliance, risk reduction, and operational continuity across construction, oil &
gas, manufacturing, facilities management, and other high-risk sectors in the UAE and
beyond.
In addition to consultancy and training, COTER Global provides specialized recruitment
services for qualified Occupational Health and Safety (OHSE) professionals, including HSE
Managers, Engineers, Officers, and Advisors. Our recruitment division focuses on
connecting top-tier safety professionals with leading organizations, ensuring the right
expertise is deployed to meet project and corporate HSE requirements effectively.
Cover About Us Services Contact Us

Cover About Us Services Contact Us
OUR MISSION
To empower industries by delivering
specialized recruitment solutions that
connect them with qualified Occupational
Health, Safety, and Environment (OHSE)
professionals, helping organizations build
safer, compliant, and more resilient
workplaces.
OUR VISION
To be a global leader in specialized HSE
recruitment, recognized for connecting
industries with top Occupational Health
and Safety professionals and contributing
to safer, more sustainable, and high-
performing workplaces worldwide.

At COTER Global, our people are more than professionals - they are safety and business partners.

We recruit qualified HSE professionals with proven expertise in safety, compliance, and
environmental management — covering all positions from HSE Assistants to OHSE Directors.
Our candidates are ready to integrate seamlessly into your operations, delivering immediate
value by strengthening safety culture, sustainability, and overall performance.

Additional Information



Candidate  Screening  Interview  
 
Executive  Summary:   This  quick  screening  interview  is  designed  to  assess  candidate  seriousness,  
availability,
 
and
 
reliability
 
within
 
5
 
minutes.
 
Use
 
this
 
checklist
 
before
 
forwarding
 
candidates
 
to
 
clients.
 
Questions:  
1.  Are  you  currently  working?  If  yes,  have  you  resigned?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I  have  resigned"  or  "No,  I’m  available  
immediately"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "Still  working  but  haven’t  informed  my  employer"  
 2.  What  is  your  exact  joining  availability?  a.  Expected  Answer:  A  speciﬁc  date  within  the  required  timeline,  example:  
"I
 
can
 
join
 
on
 
or
 
before
 
5th
 
August"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "It  depends..."  or  vague  responses  
 3.  Have  you  discussed  this  opportunity  with  your  family  or  dependents?  Are  they  
supportive?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  they  support  my  decision"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Not  yet"  or  visible  hesitation  
 4.  Have  you  applied  elsewhere  or  do  you  have  other  offers  pending?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "No,  I  am  focused  on  this  opportunity"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Yes,  I  have  multiple  offers  and  waiting  to  decide"  
 5.  Are  you  fully  committed  to  joining  this  job  if  selected?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  100%  committed"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  conﬁrm  after  selection"  or  uncertainty

6.  Are  you  ready  to  relocate  and  work  under  the  offered  conditions  
(accommodation,
 
food,
 
shifts)?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I’m  okay  with  the  terms"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  see  after  selection"  or  conditional  acceptance  
 7.  Are  your  documents  ready  —  valid  passport,  certiﬁcates,  etc.?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  all  documents  are  ready"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I  need  to  arrange  them"  or  "Not  sure  if  all  are  valid"  
 
Wrap-Up  Line:   
“Thanks.
 
If
 
selected,
 
would
 
you
 
be
 
willing
 
to
 
sign
 
a
 
short
 
commitment
 
letter
 
conﬁrming
 
your
 
intent
 
to
 
join?”
 
(This
 
is
 
not
 
legally
 
binding,
 
but
 
it
 
helps
 
reinforce
 
commitment.)

About Us
Who We Are
COTER Global is a specialized Health, Safety & Environment (HSE) consultancy, training,
and recruitment firm dedicated to helping organizations build safer workplaces. We deliver
industry-aligned safety solutions, accredited training, and experienced HSE personnel to
support compliance, risk reduction, and operational continuity across construction, oil &
gas, manufacturing, facilities management, and other high-risk sectors in the UAE and
beyond.
In addition to consultancy and training, COTER Global provides specialized recruitment
services for qualified Occupational Health and Safety (OHSE) professionals, including HSE
Managers, Engineers, Officers, and Advisors. Our recruitment division focuses on
connecting top-tier safety professionals with leading organizations, ensuring the right
expertise is deployed to meet project and corporate HSE requirements effectively.

Additional Information



Candidate  Screening  Interview  
 
Executive  Summary:   This  quick  screening  interview  is  designed  to  assess  candidate  seriousness,  
availability,
 
and
 
reliability
 
within
 
5
 
minutes.
 
Use
 
this
 
checklist
 
before
 
forwarding
 
candidates
 
to
 
clients.
 
Questions:  
1.  Are  you  currently  working?  If  yes,  have  you  resigned?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I  have  resigned"  or  "No,  I’m  available  
immediately"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "Still  working  but  haven’t  informed  my  employer"  
 2.  What  is  your  exact  joining  availability?  a.  Expected  Answer:  A  speciﬁc  date  within  the  required  timeline,  example:  
"I
 
can
 
join
 
on
 
or
 
before
 
5th
 
August"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "It  depends..."  or  vague  responses  
 3.  Have  you  discussed  this  opportunity  with  your  family  or  dependents?  Are  they  
supportive?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  they  support  my  decision"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Not  yet"  or  visible  hesitation  
 4.  Have  you  applied  elsewhere  or  do  you  have  other  offers  pending?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "No,  I  am  focused  on  this  opportunity"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Yes,  I  have  multiple  offers  and  waiting  to  decide"  
 5.  Are  you  fully  committed  to  joining  this  job  if  selected?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  100%  committed"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  conﬁrm  after  selection"  or  uncertainty

6.  Are  you  ready  to  relocate  and  work  under  the  offered  conditions  
(accommodation,
 
food,
 
shifts)?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I’m  okay  with  the  terms"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  see  after  selection"  or  conditional  acceptance  
 7.  Are  your  documents  ready  —  valid  passport,  certiﬁcates,  etc.?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  all  documents  are  ready"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I  need  to  arrange  them"  or  "Not  sure  if  all  are  valid"  
 
Wrap-Up  Line:

About Us
Who We Are
COTER Global is a specialized Health, Safety & Environment (HSE) consultancy, training,
and recruitment firm dedicated to helping organizations build safer workplaces. We deliver
industry-aligned safety solutions, accredited training, and experienced HSE personnel to
support compliance, risk reduction, and operational continuity across construction, oil &
gas, manufacturing, facilities management, and other high-risk sectors in the UAE and
beyond.
In addition to consultancy and training, COTER Global provides specialized recruitment
services for qualified Occupational Health and Safety (OHSE) professionals, including HSE
Managers, Engineers, Officers, and Advisors. Our recruitment division focuses on
connecting top-tier safety professionals with leading organizations, ensuring the right
expertise is deployed to meet project and corporate HSE requirements effectively.
Cover About Us Services Contact Us

Cover About Us Services Contact Us
OUR MISSION
To empower industries by delivering
specialized recruitment solutions that
connect them with qualified Occupational
Health, Safety, and Environment (OHSE)
professionals, helping organizations build
safer, compliant, and more resilient
workplaces.
OUR VISION
To be a global leader in specialized HSE
recruitment, recognized for connecting
industries with top Occupational Health
and Safety professionals and contributing
to safer, more sustainable, and high-
performing workplaces worldwide.

Meet Our Team
At COTER Global, our people are more than professionals - they are safety and business partners.  
Together, they deliver reliable expertise that protects, empowers, and grows your workforce.

We recruit qualified HSE professionals with proven expertise in safety, compliance, and
environmental management — covering all positions from HSE Assistants to OHSE Directors.
Our candidates are ready to integrate seamlessly into your operations, delivering immediate
value by strengthening safety culture, sustainability, and overall performance.

Additional Information



Candidate  Screening  Interview  
 
Executive  Summary:   This  quick  screening  interview  is  designed  to  assess  candidate  seriousness,  
availability,
 
and
 
reliability
 
within
 
5
 
minutes.
 
Use
 
this
 
checklist
 
before
 
forwarding
 
candidates
 
to
 
clients.
 
Questions:  
1.  Are  you  currently  working?  If  yes,  have  you  resigned?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I  have  resigned"  or  "No,  I’m  available  
immediately"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "Still  working  but  haven’t  informed  my  employer"  
 2.  What  is  your  exact  joining  availability?  a.  Expected  Answer:  A  speciﬁc  date  within  the  required  timeline,  example:  
"I
 
can
 
join
 
on
 
or
 
before
 
5th
 
August"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "It  depends..."  or  vague  responses  
 3.  Have  you  discussed  this  opportunity  with  your  family  or  dependents?  Are  they  
supportive?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  they  support  my  decision"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Not  yet"  or  visible  hesitation  
 4.  Have  you  applied  elsewhere  or  do  you  have  other  offers  pending?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "No,  I  am  focused  on  this  opportunity"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Yes,  I  have  multiple  offers  and  waiting  to  decide"  
 5.  Are  you  fully  committed  to  joining  this  job  if  selected?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  100%  committed"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  conﬁrm  after  selection"  or  uncertainty

6.  Are  you  ready  to  relocate  and  work  under  the  offered  conditions  
(accommodation,
 
food,
 
shifts)?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I’m  okay  with  the  terms"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  see  after  selection"  or  conditional  acceptance  
 7.  Are  your  documents  ready  —  valid  passport,  certiﬁcates,  etc.?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  all  documents  are  ready"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I  need  to  arrange  them"  or  "Not  sure  if  all  are  valid"  
 
Wrap-Up  Line:   
“Thanks.
 
If
 
selected,
 
would
 
you
 
be
 
willing
 
to
 
sign
 
a
 
short
 
commitment
 
letter
 
conﬁrming
 
your
 
intent
 
to
 
join?”

it
 
helps

commitment.)

About Us
Who We Are
COTER Global is a specialized Health, Safety & Environment (HSE) consultancy, training,
and recruitment firm dedicated to helping organizations build safer workplaces. We deliver
industry-aligned safety solutions, accredited training, and experienced HSE personnel to
support compliance, risk reduction, and operational continuity across construction, oil &
gas, manufacturing, facilities management, and other high-risk sectors in the UAE and
beyond.
In addition to consultancy and training, COTER Global provides specialized recruitment
services for qualified Occupational Health and Safety (OHSE) professionals, including HSE
Managers, Engineers, Officers, and Advisors. Our recruitment division focuses on
connecting top-tier safety professionals with leading organizations, ensuring the right
expertise is deployed to meet project and corporate HSE requirements effectively.
Cover About Us Services Contact Us

Cover About Us Services Contact Us
OUR MISSION
To empower industries by delivering
specialized recruitment solutions that
connect them with qualified Occupational
Health, Safety, and Environment (OHSE)
professionals, helping organizations build
safer, compliant, and more resilient
workplaces.
OUR VISION
To be a global leader in specialized HSE
recruitment, recognized for connecting
industries with top Occupational Health
and Safety professionals and contributing
to safer, more sustainable, and high-
performing workplaces worldwide.

Meet Our Team
At COTER Global, our people are more than professionals - they are safety and business partners.  
Together, they deliver reliable expertise that protects, empowers, and grows your workforce.

We recruit qualified HSE professionals with proven expertise in safety, compliance, and
environmental management — covering all positions from HSE Assistants to OHSE Directors.
Our candidates are ready to integrate seamlessly into your operations, delivering immediate
value by strengthening safety culture, sustainability, and overall performance.

availability,
 
and
 
reliability
 
within
 
5
 
minutes.

this
 
checklist
 
before
 
forwarding
 
candidates
 
to
 
clients.

immediately"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "Still  working  but  haven’t  informed  my  employer"  
 2.  What  is  your  exact  joining  availability?  a.  Expected  Answer:  A  speciﬁc  date  within  the  required  timeline,  example:  
"I
 
can
 
join
 
on
 
or
 
before
 
5th
 
August"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "It  depends..."  or  vague  responses  
 3.  Have  you  discussed  this  opportunity  with  your  family  or  dependents?  Are  they  
supportive?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  they  support  my  decision"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Not  yet"  or  visible  hesitation  
 4.  Have  you  applied  elsewhere  or  do  you  have  other  offers  pending?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "No,  I  am  focused  on  this  opportunity"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Yes,  I  have  multiple  offers  and  waiting  to  decide"

6.  Are  you  ready  to  relocate  and  work  under  the  offered  conditions  
(accommodation,
 
food,
 
shifts)?

Additional Information



Candidate  Screening  Interview  
 
Executive  Summary:   This  quick  screening  interview  is  designed  to  assess  candidate  seriousness,  
availability,
 
and
 
reliability
 
within
 
5
 
minutes.
 
Use
 
this
 
checklist
 
before
 
forwarding
 
candidates
 
to
 
clients.
 
Questions:  
1.  Are  you  currently  working?  If  yes,  have  you  resigned?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I  have  resigned"  or  "No,  I’m  available  
immediately"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "Still  working  but  haven’t  informed  my  employer"  
 2.  What  is  your  exact  joining  availability?  a.  Expected  Answer:  A  speciﬁc  date  within  the  required  timeline,  example:  
"I
 
can
 
join
 
on
 
or
 
before
 
5th
 
August"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "It  depends..."  or  vague  responses  
 3.  Have  you  discussed  this  opportunity  with  your  family  or  dependents?  Are  they  
supportive?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  they  support  my  decision"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Not  yet"  or  visible  hesitation  
 4.  Have  you  applied  elsewhere  or  do  you  have  other  offers  pending?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "No,  I  am  focused  on  this  opportunity"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Yes,  I  have  multiple  offers  and  waiting  to  decide"  
 5.  Are  you  fully  committed  to  joining  this  job  if  selected?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  100%  committed"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  conﬁrm  after  selection"  or  uncertainty

6.  Are  you  ready  to  relocate  and  work  under  the  offered  conditions  
(accommodation,
 
food,
 
shifts)?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I’m  okay  with  the  terms"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  see  after  selection"  or  conditional  acceptance  
 7.  Are  your  documents  ready  —  valid  passport,  certiﬁcates,  etc.?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  all  documents  are  ready"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I  need  to  arrange  them"  or  "Not  sure  if  all  are  valid"  
 
Wrap-Up  Line:   
“Thanks.
 
If
 
selected,
 
would
 
you
 
be
 
willing
 
to

a
 
short
 
commitment
 
letter
 
conﬁrming
 
your

to

About Us
Who We Are
COTER Global is a specialized Health, Safety & Environment (HSE) consultancy, training,
and recruitment firm dedicated to helping organizations build safer workplaces. We deliver
industry-aligned safety solutions, accredited training, and experienced HSE personnel to
support compliance, risk reduction, and operational continuity across construction, oil &
gas, manufacturing, facilities management, and other high-risk sectors in the UAE and
beyond.
In addition to consultancy and training, COTER Global provides specialized recruitment
services for qualified Occupational Health and Safety (OHSE) professionals, including HSE
Managers, Engineers, Officers, and Advisors. Our recruitment division focuses on
connecting top-tier safety professionals with leading organizations, ensuring the right
expertise is deployed to meet project and corporate HSE requirements effectively.
Cover About Us Services Contact Us

Cover About Us Services Contact Us
OUR MISSION
To empower industries by delivering
specialized recruitment solutions that
connect them with qualified Occupational
Health, Safety, and Environment (OHSE)
professionals, helping organizations build
safer, compliant, and more resilient
workplaces.
OUR VISION
To be a global leader in specialized HSE
recruitment, recognized for connecting
industries with top Occupational Health
and Safety professionals and contributing
to safer, more sustainable, and high-
performing workplaces worldwide.

Meet Our Team
At COTER Global, our people are more than professionals - they are safety and business partners.  
Together, they deliver reliable expertise that protects, empowers, and grows your workforce.

We recruit qualified HSE professionals with proven expertise in safety, compliance, and
environmental management — covering all positions from HSE Assistants to OHSE Directors.
Our candidates are ready to integrate seamlessly into your operations, delivering immediate
value by strengthening safety culture, sustainability, and overall performance.

and

within

before

to

immediately"

 2.  What  is  your  exact  joining  availability?  a.  Expected  Answer:  A  speciﬁc  date  within  the  required  timeline,  example:  
"I
 
can
 
join
 
on
 
or
 
before
 
5th
 
August"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "It  depends..."  or  vague  responses  
 3.  Have  you  discussed  this  opportunity  with  your  family  or  dependents?  Are  they  
supportive?

6.  Are  you  ready  to  relocate  and  work  under  the  offered  conditions  
(accommodation,
 
food,
 
shifts)?

 7.  Are  your  documents  ready  —  valid  passport,  certiﬁcates,  etc.?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  all  documents  are  ready"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I  need  to  arrange  them"  or  "Not  sure  if  all  are  valid"

COTER Global is a specialized Health, Safety & Environment (HSE) consultancy, training,
and recruitment firm dedicated to helping organizations build safer workplaces. We deliver
industry-aligned safety solutions, accredited training, and experienced HSE personnel to
support compliance, risk reduction, and operational continuity across construction, oil &
gas, manufacturing, facilities management, and other high-risk sectors in the UAE and
beyond.
In addition to consultancy and training, COTER Global provides specialized recruitment
services for qualified Occupational Health and Safety (OHSE) professionals, including HSE
Managers, Engineers, Officers, and Advisors. Our recruitment division focuses on
connecting top-tier safety professionals with leading organizations, ensuring the right
expertise is deployed to meet project and corporate HSE requirements effectively.

workplaces.
OUR VISION
To be a global leader in specialized HSE
recruitment, recognized for connecting
industries with top Occupational Health
and Safety professionals and contributing
to safer, more sustainable, and high-
performing workplaces worldwide.

Meet Our Team
At COTER Global, our people are more than professionals - they are safety and business partners.  
Together, they deliver reliable expertise that protects, empowers, and grows your workforce.

We recruit qualified HSE professionals with proven expertise in safety, compliance, and
environmental management — covering all positions from HSE Assistants to OHSE Directors.
Our candidates are ready to integrate seamlessly into your operations, delivering immediate
value by strengthening safety culture, sustainability, and overall performance.

Additional Information



Candidate  Screening  Interview  
 
Executive  Summary:   This  quick  screening  interview  is  designed  to  assess  candidate  seriousness,  
availability,
 
and
 
reliability
 
within
 
5
 
minutes.
 
Use
 
this
 
checklist
 
before
 
forwarding
 
candidates
 
to
 
clients.
 
Questions:  
1.  Are  you  currently  working?  If  yes,  have  you  resigned?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I  have  resigned"  or  "No,  I’m  available  
immediately"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "Still  working  but  haven’t  informed  my  employer"  
 2.  What  is  your  exact  joining  availability?  a.  Expected  Answer:  A  speciﬁc  date  within  the  required  timeline,  example:  
"I
 
can
 
join
 
on
 
or
 
before
 
5th
 
August"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "It  depends..."  or  vague  responses  
 3.  Have  you  discussed  this  opportunity  with  your  family  or  dependents?  Are  they  
supportive?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  they  support  my  decision"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Not  yet"  or  visible  hesitation  
 4.  Have  you  applied  elsewhere  or  do  you  have  other  offers  pending?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "No,  I  am  focused  on  this  opportunity"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Yes,  I  have  multiple  offers  and  waiting  to  decide"  
 5.  Are  you  fully  committed  to  joining  this  job  if  selected?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  100%  committed"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  conﬁrm  after  selection"  or  uncertainty

6.  Are  you  ready  to  relocate  and  work  under  the  offered  conditions  
(accommodation,
 
food,
 
shifts)?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I’m  okay  with  the  terms"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  see  after  selection"  or  conditional  acceptance  
 7.  Are  your  documents  ready  —  valid  passport,  certiﬁcates,  etc.?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  all  documents  are  ready"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I  need  to  arrange  them"  or  "Not  sure  if  all  are  valid"  
 
Wrap-Up  Line:   
“Thanks.
 
If
 
selected,
 
would
 
you
 
be
 
willing
 
to
 
sign
 
a
 
short
 
commitment
 
letter
 
conﬁrming
 
your
 
intent
 
to
 
join?”
 
(This
 
is
 
not
 
legally
 
binding,
 
but
 
it
 
helps
 
reinforce
 
commitment.)

COTER  Global  Candidate  Commitment  Letter

About Us
Who We Are
COTER Global is a specialized Health, Safety & Environment (HSE) consultancy, training,
and recruitment firm dedicated to helping organizations build safer workplaces. We deliver
industry-aligned safety solutions, accredited training, and experienced HSE personnel to
support compliance, risk reduction, and operational continuity across construction, oil &
gas, manufacturing, facilities management, and other high-risk sectors in the UAE and
beyond.
In addition to consultancy and training, COTER Global provides specialized recruitment
services for qualified Occupational Health and Safety (OHSE) professionals, including HSE
Managers, Engineers, Officers, and Advisors. Our recruitment division focuses on
connecting top-tier safety professionals with leading organizations, ensuring the right
expertise is deployed to meet project and corporate HSE requirements effectively.
Cover About Us Services Contact Us

Cover About Us Services Contact Us
OUR MISSION
To empower industries by delivering
specialized recruitment solutions that
connect them with qualified Occupational
Health, Safety, and Environment (OHSE)
professionals, helping organizations build
safer, compliant, and more resilient
workplaces.
OUR VISION
To be a global leader in specialized HSE
recruitment, recognized for connecting
industries with top Occupational Health
and Safety professionals and contributing
to safer, more sustainable, and high-
performing workplaces worldwide.

At COTER Global, our people are more than professionals - they are safety and business partners.  
Together, they deliver reliable expertise that protects, empowers, and grows your workforce.

We recruit qualified HSE professionals with proven expertise in safety, compliance, and
environmental management — covering all positions from HSE Assistants to OHSE Directors.
Our candidates are ready to integrate seamlessly into your operations, delivering immediate
value by strengthening safety culture, sustainability, and overall performance.

Candidate  Screening  Interview  
 
Executive  Summary:   This  quick  screening  interview  is  designed  to  assess  candidate  seriousness,  
availability,
 
and
 
reliability
 
within
 
5
 
minutes.
 
Use
 
this
 
checklist
 
before
 
forwarding
 
candidates
 
to
 
clients.

1.  Are  you  currently  working?  If  yes,  have  you  resigned?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I  have  resigned"  or  "No,  I’m  available  
immediately"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "Still  working  but  haven’t  informed  my  employer"  
 2.  What  is  your  exact  joining  availability?  a.  Expected  Answer:  A  speciﬁc  date  within  the  required  timeline,  example:  
"I
 
can
 
join
 
on
 
or
 
before
 
5th
 
August"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "It  depends..."  or  vague  responses  
 3.  Have  you  discussed  this  opportunity  with  your  family  or  dependents?  Are  they  
supportive?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  they  support  my  decision"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Not  yet"  or  visible  hesitation  
 4.  Have  you  applied  elsewhere  or  do  you  have  other  offers  pending?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "No,  I  am  focused  on  this  opportunity"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Yes,  I  have  multiple  offers  and  waiting  to  decide"  
 5.  Are  you  fully  committed  to  joining  this  job  if  selected?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  100%  committed"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  conﬁrm  after  selection"  or  uncertainty

6.  Are  you  ready  to  relocate  and  work  under  the  offered  conditions  
(accommodation,
 
food,
 
shifts)?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I’m  okay  with  the  terms"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  see  after  selection"  or  conditional  acceptance  
 7.  Are  your  documents  ready  —  valid  passport,  certiﬁcates,  etc.?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  all  documents  are  ready"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I  need  to  arrange  them"  or  "Not  sure  if  all  are  valid"

About Us
Who We Are
COTER Global is a specialized Health, Safety & Environment (HSE) consultancy, training,
and recruitment firm dedicated to helping organizations build safer workplaces. We deliver
industry-aligned safety solutions, accredited training, and experienced HSE personnel to
support compliance, risk reduction, and operational continuity across construction, oil &
gas, manufacturing, facilities management, and other high-risk sectors in the UAE and
beyond.
In addition to consultancy and training, COTER Global provides specialized recruitment
services for qualified Occupational Health and Safety (OHSE) professionals, including HSE
Managers, Engineers, Officers, and Advisors. Our recruitment division focuses on
connecting top-tier safety professionals with leading organizations, ensuring the right
expertise is deployed to meet project and corporate HSE requirements effectively.
Cover About Us Services Contact Us

Cover About Us Services Contact Us
OUR MISSION
To empower industries by delivering
specialized recruitment solutions that
connect them with qualified Occupational
Health, Safety, and Environment (OHSE)
professionals, helping organizations build
safer, compliant, and more resilient
workplaces.
OUR VISION
To be a global leader in specialized HSE
recruitment, recognized for connecting
industries with top Occupational Health
and Safety professionals and contributing
to safer, more sustainable, and high-
performing workplaces worldwide.

Meet Our Team
At COTER Global, our people are more than professionals - they are safety and business partners.  
Together, they deliver reliable expertise that protects, empowers, and grows your workforce.

We recruit qualified HSE professionals with proven expertise in safety, compliance, and
environmental management — covering all positions from HSE Assistants to OHSE Directors.
Our candidates are ready to integrate seamlessly into your operations, delivering immediate
value by strengthening safety culture, sustainability, and overall performance.

Additional Information



Candidate  Screening  Interview  
 
Executive  Summary:   This  quick  screening  interview  is  designed  to  assess  candidate  seriousness,  
availability,
 
and
 
reliability
 
within
 
5
 
minutes.
 
Use
 
this
 
checklist
 
before
 
forwarding
 
candidates
 
to
 
clients.
 
Questions:  
1.  Are  you  currently  working?  If  yes,  have  you  resigned?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I  have  resigned"  or  "No,  I’m  available  
immediately"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "Still  working  but  haven’t  informed  my  employer"  
 2.  What  is  your  exact  joining  availability?  a.  Expected  Answer:  A  speciﬁc  date  within  the  required  timeline,  example:  
"I
 
can
 
join
 
on
 
or
 
before
 
5th
 
August"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "It  depends..."  or  vague  responses  
 3.  Have  you  discussed  this  opportunity  with  your  family  or  dependents?  Are  they  
supportive?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  they  support  my  decision"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Not  yet"  or  visible  hesitation  
 4.  Have  you  applied  elsewhere  or  do  you  have  other  offers  pending?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "No,  I  am  focused  on  this  opportunity"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Yes,  I  have  multiple  offers  and  waiting  to  decide"  
 5.  Are  you  fully  committed  to  joining  this  job  if  selected?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  100%  committed"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  conﬁrm  after  selection"  or  uncertainty

6.  Are  you  ready  to  relocate  and  work  under  the  offered  conditions  
(accommodation,
 
food,
 
shifts)?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I’m  okay  with  the  terms"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  see  after  selection"  or  conditional  acceptance  
 7.  Are  your  documents  ready  —  valid  passport,  certiﬁcates,  etc.?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  all  documents  are  ready"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I  need  to  arrange  them"  or  "Not  sure  if  all  are  valid"  
 
Wrap-Up  Line:   
“Thanks.
 
If
 
selected,
 
would
 
you
 
be
 
willing
 
to
 
sign
 
a
 
short
 
commitment
 
letter
 
conﬁrming
 
your
 
intent
 
to
 
join?”
 
(This
 
is
 
not
 
legally
 
binding,
 
but
 
it
 
helps
 
reinforce
 
commitment.)

COTER Global is a specialized Health, Safety & Environment (HSE) consultancy, training,
and recruitment firm dedicated to helping organizations build safer workplaces. We deliver
industry-aligned safety solutions, accredited training, and experienced HSE personnel to
support compliance, risk reduction, and operational continuity across construction, oil &
gas, manufacturing, facilities management, and other high-risk sectors in the UAE and
beyond.
In addition to consultancy and training, COTER Global provides specialized recruitment
services for qualified Occupational Health and Safety (OHSE) professionals, including HSE
Managers, Engineers, Officers, and Advisors. Our recruitment division focuses on
connecting top-tier safety professionals with leading organizations, ensuring the right
expertise is deployed to meet project and corporate HSE requirements effectively.

Additional Information



Candidate  Screening  Interview  
 
Executive  Summary:   This  quick  screening  interview  is  designed  to  assess  candidate  seriousness,  
availability,
 
and
 
reliability
 
within
 
5
 
minutes.
 
Use
 
this
 
checklist
 
before
 
forwarding
 
candidates
 
to
 
clients.
 
Questions:  
1.  Are  you  currently  working?  If  yes,  have  you  resigned?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I  have  resigned"  or  "No,  I’m  available  
immediately"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "Still  working  but  haven’t  informed  my  employer"  
 2.  What  is  your  exact  joining  availability?  a.  Expected  Answer:  A  speciﬁc  date  within  the  required  timeline,  example:  
"I
 
can
 
join
 
on
 
or
 
before
 
5th
 
August"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "It  depends..."  or  vague  responses  
 3.  Have  you  discussed  this  opportunity  with  your  family  or  dependents?  Are  they  
supportive?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  they  support  my  decision"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Not  yet"  or  visible  hesitation  
 4.  Have  you  applied  elsewhere  or  do  you  have  other  offers  pending?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "No,  I  am  focused  on  this  opportunity"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Yes,  I  have  multiple  offers  and  waiting  to  decide"  
 5.  Are  you  fully  committed  to  joining  this  job  if  selected?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  100%  committed"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  conﬁrm  after  selection"  or  uncertainty

6.  Are  you  ready  to  relocate  and  work  under  the  offered  conditions  
(accommodation,
 
food,
 
shifts)?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I’m  okay  with  the  terms"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  see  after  selection"  or  conditional  acceptance  
 7.  Are  your  documents  ready  —  valid  passport,  certiﬁcates,  etc.?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  all  documents  are  ready"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I  need  to  arrange  them"  or  "Not  sure  if  all  are  valid"  
 
Wrap-Up  Line:   
“Thanks.
 
If
 
selected,
 
would
 
you
 
be
 
willing
 
to
 
sign
 
a
 
short
 
commitment
 
letter
 
conﬁrming
 
your
 
intent
 
to
 
join?”

About Us
Who We Are
COTER Global is a specialized Health, Safety & Environment (HSE) consultancy, training,
and recruitment firm dedicated to helping organizations build safer workplaces. We deliver
industry-aligned safety solutions, accredited training, and experienced HSE personnel to
support compliance, risk reduction, and operational continuity across construction, oil &
gas, manufacturing, facilities management, and other high-risk sectors in the UAE and
beyond.
In addition to consultancy and training, COTER Global provides specialized recruitment
services for qualified Occupational Health and Safety (OHSE) professionals, including HSE
Managers, Engineers, Officers, and Advisors. Our recruitment division focuses on
connecting top-tier safety professionals with leading organizations, ensuring the right
expertise is deployed to meet project and corporate HSE requirements effectively.
Cover About Us Services Contact Us

Cover About Us Services Contact Us
OUR MISSION
To empower industries by delivering
specialized recruitment solutions that
connect them with qualified Occupational
Health, Safety, and Environment (OHSE)
professionals, helping organizations build
safer, compliant, and more resilient
workplaces.
OUR VISION
To be a global leader in specialized HSE
recruitment, recognized for connecting
industries with top Occupational Health
and Safety professionals and contributing
to safer, more sustainable, and high-
performing workplaces worldwide.

Meet Our Team
At COTER Global, our people are more than professionals - they are safety and business partners.  
Together, they deliver reliable expertise that protects, empowers, and grows your workforce.

We recruit qualified HSE professionals with proven expertise in safety, compliance, and
environmental management — covering all positions from HSE Assistants to OHSE Directors.
Our candidates are ready to integrate seamlessly into your operations, delivering immediate
value by strengthening safety culture, sustainability, and overall performance.

Candidate  Screening  Interview  
 
Executive  Summary:   This  quick  screening  interview  is  designed  to  assess  candidate  seriousness,  
availability,
 
and
 
reliability
 
within
 
5
 
minutes.
 
Use
 
this
 
checklist
 
before
 
forwarding
 
candidates
 
to
 
clients.
 
Questions:  
1.  Are  you  currently  working?  If  yes,  have  you  resigned?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I  have  resigned"  or  "No,  I’m  available  
immediately"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "Still  working  but  haven’t  informed  my  employer"  
 2.  What  is  your  exact  joining  availability?  a.  Expected  Answer:  A  speciﬁc  date  within  the  required  timeline,  example:  
"I
 
can
 
join
 
on
 
or
 
before
 
5th
 
August"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "It  depends..."  or  vague  responses  
 3.  Have  you  discussed  this  opportunity  with  your  family  or  dependents?  Are  they  
supportive?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  they  support  my  decision"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Not  yet"  or  visible  hesitation  
 4.  Have  you  applied  elsewhere  or  do  you  have  other  offers  pending?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "No,  I  am  focused  on  this  opportunity"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Yes,  I  have  multiple  offers  and  waiting  to  decide"  
 5.  Are  you  fully  committed  to  joining  this  job  if  selected?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  100%  committed"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  conﬁrm  after  selection"  or  uncertainty

6.  Are  you  ready  to  relocate  and  work  under  the  offered  conditions  
(accommodation,
 
food,
 
shifts)?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I’m  okay  with  the  terms"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  see  after  selection"  or  conditional  acceptance  
 7.  Are  your  documents  ready  —  valid  passport,  certiﬁcates,  etc.?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  all  documents  are  ready"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I  need  to  arrange  them"  or  "Not  sure  if  all  are  valid"

About Us
Who We Are
COTER Global is a specialized Health, Safety & Environment (HSE) consultancy, training,
and recruitment firm dedicated to helping organizations build safer workplaces. We deliver
industry-aligned safety solutions, accredited training, and experienced HSE personnel to
support compliance, risk reduction, and operational continuity across construction, oil &
gas, manufacturing, facilities management, and other high-risk sectors in the UAE and
beyond.
In addition to consultancy and training, COTER Global provides specialized recruitment
services for qualified Occupational Health and Safety (OHSE) professionals, including HSE
Managers, Engineers, Officers, and Advisors. Our recruitment division focuses on
connecting top-tier safety professionals with leading organizations, ensuring the right
expertise is deployed to meet project and corporate HSE requirements effectively.

Additional Information



Candidate  Screening  Interview  
 
Executive  Summary:   This  quick  screening  interview  is  designed  to  assess  candidate  seriousness,  
availability,
 
and
 
reliability
 
within
 
5
 
minutes.
 
Use
 
this
 
checklist
 
before
 
forwarding
 
candidates
 
to
 
clients.
 
Questions:  
1.  Are  you  currently  working?  If  yes,  have  you  resigned?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I  have  resigned"  or  "No,  I’m  available  
immediately"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "Still  working  but  haven’t  informed  my  employer"  
 2.  What  is  your  exact  joining  availability?  a.  Expected  Answer:  A  speciﬁc  date  within  the  required  timeline,  example:  
"I
 
can
 
join
 
on
 
or
 
before
 
5th
 
August"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "It  depends..."  or  vague  responses  
 3.  Have  you  discussed  this  opportunity  with  your  family  or  dependents?  Are  they  
supportive?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  they  support  my  decision"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Not  yet"  or  visible  hesitation  
 4.  Have  you  applied  elsewhere  or  do  you  have  other  offers  pending?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "No,  I  am  focused  on  this  opportunity"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Yes,  I  have  multiple  offers  and  waiting  to  decide"  
 5.  Are  you  fully  committed  to  joining  this  job  if  selected?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  100%  committed"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  conﬁrm  after  selection"  or  uncertainty

6.  Are  you  ready  to  relocate  and  work  under  the  offered  conditions  
(accommodation,
 
food,
 
shifts)?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I’m  okay  with  the  terms"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  see  after  selection"  or  conditional  acceptance  
 7.  Are  your  documents  ready  —  valid  passport,  certiﬁcates,  etc.?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  all  documents  are  ready"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I  need  to  arrange  them"  or  "Not  sure  if  all  are  valid"  
 
Wrap-Up  Line:   
“Thanks.
 
If
 
selected,
 
would
 
you
 
be
 
willing
 
to
 
sign
 
a
 
short
 
commitment
 
letter
 
conﬁrming
 
your
 
intent
 
to
 
join?”

About Us
Who We Are
COTER Global is a specialized Health, Safety & Environment (HSE) consultancy, training,
and recruitment firm dedicated to helping organizations build safer workplaces. We deliver
industry-aligned safety solutions, accredited training, and experienced HSE personnel to
support compliance, risk reduction, and operational continuity across construction, oil &
gas, manufacturing, facilities management, and other high-risk sectors in the UAE and
beyond.
In addition to consultancy and training, COTER Global provides specialized recruitment
services for qualified Occupational Health and Safety (OHSE) professionals, including HSE
Managers, Engineers, Officers, and Advisors. Our recruitment division focuses on
connecting top-tier safety professionals with leading organizations, ensuring the right
expertise is deployed to meet project and corporate HSE requirements effectively.
Cover About Us Services Contact Us

Cover About Us Services Contact Us
OUR MISSION
To empower industries by delivering
specialized recruitment solutions that
connect them with qualified Occupational
Health, Safety, and Environment (OHSE)
professionals, helping organizations build
safer, compliant, and more resilient
workplaces.
OUR VISION
To be a global leader in specialized HSE
recruitment, recognized for connecting
industries with top Occupational Health
and Safety professionals and contributing
to safer, more sustainable, and high-
performing workplaces worldwide.

Meet Our Team
At COTER Global, our people are more than professionals - they are safety and business partners.  
Together, they deliver reliable expertise that protects, empowers, and grows your workforce.

We recruit qualified HSE professionals with proven expertise in safety, compliance, and
environmental management — covering all positions from HSE Assistants to OHSE Directors.
Our candidates are ready to integrate seamlessly into your operations, delivering immediate
value by strengthening safety culture, sustainability, and overall performance.

Meet Our Team

Together, they deliver reliable expertise that protects, empowers, and grows your workforce.

We recruit qualified HSE professionals with proven expertise in safety, compliance, and
environmental management — covering all positions from HSE Assistants to OHSE Directors.
Our candidates are ready to integrate seamlessly into your operations, delivering immediate
value by strengthening safety culture, sustainability, and overall performance.

Candidate  Screening  Interview  
 
Executive  Summary:   This  quick  screening  interview  is  designed  to  assess  candidate  seriousness,  
availability,
 
and
 
reliability
 
within
 
5
 
minutes.
 
Use
 
this
 
checklist
 
before
 
forwarding
 
candidates
 
to
 
clients.
 
Questions:  
1.  Are  you  currently  working?  If  yes,  have  you  resigned?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I  have  resigned"  or  "No,  I’m  available  
immediately"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "Still  working  but  haven’t  informed  my  employer"  
 2.  What  is  your  exact  joining  availability?  a.  Expected  Answer:  A  speciﬁc  date  within  the  required  timeline,  example:  
"I
 
can
 
join
 
on
 
or
 
before
 
5th
 
August"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "It  depends..."  or  vague  responses  
 3.  Have  you  discussed  this  opportunity  with  your  family  or  dependents?  Are  they  
supportive?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  they  support  my  decision"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Not  yet"  or  visible  hesitation  
 4.  Have  you  applied  elsewhere  or  do  you  have  other  offers  pending?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "No,  I  am  focused  on  this  opportunity"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Yes,  I  have  multiple  offers  and  waiting  to  decide"  
 5.  Are  you  fully  committed  to  joining  this  job  if  selected?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  100%  committed"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  conﬁrm  after  selection"  or  uncertainty

6.  Are  you  ready  to  relocate  and  work  under  the  offered  conditions  
(accommodation,
 
food,
 
shifts)?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I’m  okay  with  the  terms"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  see  after  selection"  or  conditional  acceptance  
 7.  Are  your  documents  ready  —  valid  passport,  certiﬁcates,  etc.?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  all  documents  are  ready"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I  need  to  arrange  them"  or  "Not  sure  if  all  are  valid"  
 
Wrap-Up  Line:   
“Thanks.
 
If
 
selected,
 
would
 
you
 
be
 
willing
 
to
 
sign
 
a
 
short
 
commitment
 
letter
 
conﬁrming
 
your
 
intent
 
to
 
join?”

legally

About Us
Who We Are
COTER Global is a specialized Health, Safety & Environment (HSE) consultancy, training,
and recruitment firm dedicated to helping organizations build safer workplaces. We deliver
industry-aligned safety solutions, accredited training, and experienced HSE personnel to
support compliance, risk reduction, and operational continuity across construction, oil &
gas, manufacturing, facilities management, and other high-risk sectors in the UAE and
beyond.
In addition to consultancy and training, COTER Global provides specialized recruitment
services for qualified Occupational Health and Safety (OHSE) professionals, including HSE
Managers, Engineers, Officers, and Advisors. Our recruitment division focuses on
connecting top-tier safety professionals with leading organizations, ensuring the right
expertise is deployed to meet project and corporate HSE requirements effectively.
Cover About Us Services Contact Us

Cover About Us Services Contact Us
OUR MISSION
To empower industries by delivering
specialized recruitment solutions that
connect them with qualified Occupational
Health, Safety, and Environment (OHSE)
professionals, helping organizations build
safer, compliant, and more resilient
workplaces.
OUR VISION
To be a global leader in specialized HSE
recruitment, recognized for connecting
industries with top Occupational Health
and Safety professionals and contributing
to safer, more sustainable, and high-
performing workplaces worldwide.

About Us
Who We Are
COTER Global is a specialized Health, Safety & Environment (HSE) consultancy, training,
and recruitment firm dedicated to helping organizations build safer workplaces. We deliver
industry-aligned safety solutions, accredited training, and experienced HSE personnel to
support compliance, risk reduction, and operational continuity across construction, oil &
gas, manufacturing, facilities management, and other high-risk sectors in the UAE and
beyond.
In addition to consultancy and training, COTER Global provides specialized recruitment
services for qualified Occupational Health and Safety (OHSE) professionals, including HSE
Managers, Engineers, Officers, and Advisors. Our recruitment division focuses on
connecting top-tier safety professionals with leading organizations, ensuring the right
expertise is deployed to meet project and corporate HSE requirements effectively.
Cover About Us Services Contact Us

Cover About Us Services Contact Us
OUR MISSION
To empower industries by delivering
specialized recruitment solutions that
connect them with qualified Occupational
Health, Safety, and Environment (OHSE)
professionals, helping organizations build
safer, compliant, and more resilient
workplaces.
OUR VISION
To be a global leader in specialized HSE
recruitment, recognized for connecting
industries with top Occupational Health
and Safety professionals and contributing
to safer, more sustainable, and high-
performing workplaces worldwide.

Additional Information



Candidate  Screening  Interview  
 
Executive  Summary:   This  quick  screening  interview  is  designed  to  assess  candidate  seriousness,  
availability,
 
and
 
reliability
 
within
 
5
 
minutes.
 
Use
 
this
 
checklist
 
before
 
forwarding
 
candidates
 
to
 
clients.
 
Questions:  
1.  Are  you  currently  working?  If  yes,  have  you  resigned?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I  have  resigned"  or  "No,  I’m  available  
immediately"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "Still  working  but  haven’t  informed  my  employer"  
 2.  What  is  your  exact  joining  availability?  a.  Expected  Answer:  A  speciﬁc  date  within  the  required  timeline,  example:  
"I
 
can
 
join
 
on
 
or
 
before
 
5th
 
August"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "It  depends..."  or  vague  responses  
 3.  Have  you  discussed  this  opportunity  with  your  family  or  dependents?  Are  they  
supportive?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  they  support  my  decision"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Not  yet"  or  visible  hesitation  
 4.  Have  you  applied  elsewhere  or  do  you  have  other  offers  pending?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "No,  I  am  focused  on  this  opportunity"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Yes,  I  have  multiple  offers  and  waiting  to  decide"  
 5.  Are  you  fully  committed  to  joining  this  job  if  selected?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  100%  committed"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  conﬁrm  after  selection"  or  uncertainty

6.  Are  you  ready  to  relocate  and  work  under  the  offered  conditions  
(accommodation,
 
food,
 
shifts)?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I’m  okay  with  the  terms"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  see  after  selection"  or  conditional  acceptance  
 7.  Are  your  documents  ready  —  valid  passport,  certiﬁcates,  etc.?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  all  documents  are  ready"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I  need  to  arrange  them"  or  "Not  sure  if  all  are  valid"  
 
Wrap-Up  Line:   
“Thanks.
 
If
 
selected,
 
would
 
you
 
be
 
willing
 
to
 
sign
 
a
 
short
 
commitment
 
letter
 
conﬁrming
 
your
 
intent
 
to
 
join?”
 
(This
 
is
 
not
 
legally
 
binding,
 
but
 
it
 
helps
 
reinforce
 
commitment.)

in
 
the
 
position
 
of

Title)

Name),

Global.

responsibilities,

and
 
location
 
associated
 
with

the

and

invested
 
in

by
 
both
 
the
 
agency
 
and
 
the

selection,
 
without
 
valid

or

notice,
 
may
 
result
 
in

proﬁle

blacklisted
 
and
 
excluded
 
from
 
future

through

I  value  professionalism,  transparency,  and  mutual  respect,  and  I  look  forward  to  
proceeding
 
with

next

expertise is deployed to meet project and corporate HSE requirements effectively.

immediately"

 2.  What  is  your  exact  joining  availability?  a.  Expected  Answer:  A  speciﬁc  date  within  the  required  timeline,  example:  
"I
 
can
 
join
 
on
 
or
 
before
 
5th
 
August"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "It  depends..."  or  vague  responses  
 3.  Have  you  discussed  this  opportunity  with  your  family  or  dependents?  Are  they  
supportive?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  they  support  my  decision"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Not  yet"  or  visible  hesitation  
 4.  Have  you  applied  elsewhere  or  do  you  have  other  offers  pending?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "No,  I  am  focused  on  this  opportunity"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Yes,  I  have  multiple  offers  and  waiting  to  decide"  
 5.  Are  you  fully  committed  to  joining  this  job  if  selected?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  100%  committed"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  conﬁrm  after  selection"  or  uncertainty

6.  Are  you  ready  to  relocate  and  work  under  the  offered  conditions  
(accommodation,
 
food,
 
shifts)?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I’m  okay  with  the  terms"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  see  after  selection"  or  conditional  acceptance  
 7.  Are  your  documents  ready  —  valid  passport,  certiﬁcates,  etc.?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  all  documents  are  ready"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I  need  to  arrange  them"  or  "Not  sure  if  all  are  valid"

About Us
Who We Are
COTER Global is a specialized Health, Safety & Environment (HSE) consultancy, training,
and recruitment firm dedicated to helping organizations build safer workplaces. We deliver
industry-aligned safety solutions, accredited training, and experienced HSE personnel to
support compliance, risk reduction, and operational continuity across construction, oil &
gas, manufacturing, facilities management, and other high-risk sectors in the UAE and
beyond.
In addition to consultancy and training, COTER Global provides specialized recruitment
services for qualified Occupational Health and Safety (OHSE) professionals, including HSE
Managers, Engineers, Officers, and Advisors. Our recruitment division focuses on
connecting top-tier safety professionals with leading organizations, ensuring the right
expertise is deployed to meet project and corporate HSE requirements effectively.
Cover About Us Services Contact Us

Cover About Us Services Contact Us
OUR MISSION
To empower industries by delivering
specialized recruitment solutions that
connect them with qualified Occupational
Health, Safety, and Environment (OHSE)
professionals, helping organizations build
safer, compliant, and more resilient
workplaces.
OUR VISION
To be a global leader in specialized HSE
recruitment, recognized for connecting
industries with top Occupational Health
and Safety professionals and contributing
to safer, more sustainable, and high-
performing workplaces worldwide.

Meet Our Team
At COTER Global, our people are more than professionals - they are safety and business partners.  
Together, they deliver reliable expertise that protects, empowers, and grows your workforce.

We recruit qualified HSE professionals with proven expertise in safety, compliance, and
environmental management — covering all positions from HSE Assistants to OHSE Directors.
Our candidates are ready to integrate seamlessly into your operations, delivering immediate
value by strengthening safety culture, sustainability, and overall performance.

Additional Information



Candidate  Screening  Interview  
 
Executive  Summary:   This  quick  screening  interview  is  designed  to  assess  candidate  seriousness,  
availability,
 
and
 
reliability
 
within
 
5
 
minutes.
 
Use
 
this
 
checklist
 
before
 
forwarding
 
candidates
 
to
 
clients.
 
Questions:  
1.  Are  you  currently  working?  If  yes,  have  you  resigned?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I  have  resigned"  or  "No,  I’m  available  
immediately"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "Still  working  but  haven’t  informed  my  employer"  
 2.  What  is  your  exact  joining  availability?  a.  Expected  Answer:  A  speciﬁc  date  within  the  required  timeline,  example:  
"I
 
can
 
join
 
on
 
or
 
before
 
5th
 
August"
 b.  Red  Flag:  "It  depends..."  or  vague  responses  
 3.  Have  you  discussed  this  opportunity  with  your  family  or  dependents?  Are  they  
supportive?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  they  support  my  decision"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Not  yet"  or  visible  hesitation  
 4.  Have  you  applied  elsewhere  or  do  you  have  other  offers  pending?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "No,  I  am  focused  on  this  opportunity"  b.  Red  Flag:  "Yes,  I  have  multiple  offers  and  waiting  to  decide"  
 5.  Are  you  fully  committed  to  joining  this  job  if  selected?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  100%  committed"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  conﬁrm  after  selection"  or  uncertainty

6.  Are  you  ready  to  relocate  and  work  under  the  offered  conditions  
(accommodation,
 
food,
 
shifts)?
 a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  I’m  okay  with  the  terms"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I’ll  see  after  selection"  or  conditional  acceptance  
 7.  Are  your  documents  ready  —  valid  passport,  certiﬁcates,  etc.?  a.  Expected  Answer:  "Yes,  all  documents  are  ready"  b.  Red  Flag:  "I  need  to  arrange  them"  or  "Not  sure  if  all  are  valid"  
 
Wrap-Up  Line:   
“Thanks.
 
If
 
selected,
 
would
 
you
 
be
 
willing
 
to
 
sign
 
a
 
short
 
commitment
 
letter
 
conﬁrming
 
your
 
intent
 
to
 
join?”
 
(This
 
is
 
not
 
legally
 
binding,
 
but
 
it
 
helps
 
reinforce
 
commitment.)

and recruitment firm dedicated to helping organizations build safer workplaces. We deliver

support compliance, risk reduction, and operational continuity across construction, oil &
gas, manufacturing, facilities management, and other high-risk sectors in the UAE and
beyond.
In addition to consultancy and training, COTER Global provides specialized recruitment

Managers, Engineers, Officers, and Advisors. Our recruitment division focuses on
connecting top-tier safety professionals with leading organizations, ensuring the right
expertise is deployed to meet project and corporate HSE requirements effectively.
